<Date>1510404442461< /Date>< Name>
Linas Bastunas< /Name>
<pics>None<//pics>< review>
Backpacker from Europe here. I got a recommendation from some locals in Sonora to come here. It was already very late when I arrived to this RV park and I had no place to stay, so I really didn't think it's a crime to pitch a tent in RV park. At 7 am got wakened up by crappy looking guy, who threatened to call police if I don't leave immediately. I explained I had no bad intentions and offered to pay for a stay with no respond. Maybe I was wrong, maybe didn't know rules or regulations, but this felt a bit of overkill at least.My late arrival to this place was not planed as it happened because I had to cancel my hiking trip from Lake Tahoe to Yosemite due to snow conditions in High Sierras. Luckily, I met plenty of nice people on my way, who gave me rides to come back to San Francisco as there was no public transportation in Sonora area. By the way, the guy who kicked me out from camping, looked like somebody who would get kicked out from many places himself.</review>

<Rate>5< /Rate>< review>
Love this gas station! Frequently go there on trips to California. They have so much more than reasonably  priced gas... It's basically a mall food court within a gas station. But that's STILL NOT ALL!!! They have  adorable souvenirs for kid's funny one's for adults and something for really everyone on your list. Car activities for every age (coloring books for children and adults // sudko and different puzzle books// card games and a few books) and Lotto tickets// Scratchers. Scratchers can be bought at the register with a cashier or at the CalLotto Box right next to the door.  ** MAKE SURE TO HAVE YOUR I.D. WITH YOU FOR YOUR PURCHASE.** At the register and at the CalLotto box the cashier will ask you at time of purchase and if you're a lucky winner you may be asked again.
Inside you can choose from so many different restaurants and tables are set up for you to sit and enjoy your meal or place it to go and head back on the road with you.
Subway
A & W
TCBY
Mrs. Field's Cookies
Pizza Hut
Or if you just need a snack the gas station itself has endless options. The hardest part of this stop on my families trip is deciding what everyone wants to eat. Employees are friendly, courteous, and very helpful. Each of the store's inside are very clean, tables and countertops are always wiped down and sanitized. The bathrooms are clean as well, plenty of stalls so there is rarely a line (for either side).

** IF COMING FOR A FOUNTAIN DRINK MAKE SURE YOU PAY FOR ONE FIRST, AT THE CASHIER'S REGISTER OR ANY OF THE RESTAURANTS ; they do not keep any cups out by the soda machine for more than likely theft... I'm assuming.**

- - - HOPE IT HELPED - - -</review>

<Review>I come here for their happy hour. They have a nice bar with great liquor choices. The craft beers on tap are well done and span a wide range of styles. They also have "guest" beers on tap, but I don't see them sell many, so I avoid those. The happy hour prices are xlnt. Mini pan pizza for $6--yes please! Plenty of screens for sports. Bartenders are fairly attentive. Place doesn't get too crazy or crowded from 3-7 usually. Friendly people at the bar. Typically a 35-55 type crowd I would guess. Great place to take a load off after shopping Brea Mall. The building has been there since the 80s I think and the interior is unique. 1525135731693</Date>
< Rating>
5< /Rating>
<Text>I like this BJ's. Every time I come here, it's packed, yet the staff do an excellent job keeping up their smiles and their service positive, not to mention excellent customer relationship management with a well designed loyalty program and complimentary guest services like free WiFi that doesn't suck.

Last time I came here was for a to-go order. It was around dinner time on a Friday, so naturally the line was out the door. I ordered ahead through their website and showed up, the to-go order counter is on the right as soon as you enter the restaurant. Informed the cashier of my name, and they went to go fetch my order from the kitchen. Within 5 minutes it was there (I guess I showed up a little early). I wanted to add a six-pack of house IPA beer to the order, and that was done seamlessly.

Thanks to the loyalty program, I had $5.00 deducted off my order (something about having customer loyalty points). Tipped the handler 20%, and left with an eagerness to consume the food ordered.

I ordered a BJ's Favorite Pizza which at the time of this review is "Housemade meatballs, pepperoni, Italian sausage, mushrooms, green bell peppers, black olives, white onions and seasoned tomatoes". It was good and I had plenty of leftovers as I ordered a medium and didn't intend to share with anyone.

Finally, a note about the technological infrastructure. I mentioned earlier that they had fast WiFi. They also have a customer loyalty program that you can tie your cell phone number to, so when you dine-in you can collect points that way. They also regularly send promotions to your email which you can collect further points that way as well as be informed of upcoming special events (like prix fixe style experiences, usually paired with some sort of excellent beer selection).

All in all, vastly impressed with BJ's and hope to be back soon. Your loyal customer, Russell.<//Text>< Pictures>
None<//Pictures>
